struct INDDATA {
   double            open[];
   double            high[];
   double            low[];
   double            close[];
   datetime          time[];
   double            tick_volume[];
   //   double            volume[];
   double            std[];
   double            stdOpen[];
   double            mfi[];
   double            obv[];
   double            rsi[];
   double            atr[];
   double            adx[];
   double            adxPlus[];
   double            adxMinus[];
   double            ima5[];
   double            ima14[];
   double            ima30[];
   double            ima60[];
   double            ima120[];
   double            ima240[];
   double            ima500[];
   ulong             magicnumber;
   double            closeProfit; // Profit at which a trade is condsidered for closing. Also the same as take profit
   double            stopLoss; // Stop Loss
   double            currProfit; // The profit of the currently held trade
   double            maxProfit; // The current profit is adjusted by subtracting the spread and a margin added.
   int               tradePosition;
   int               currSpread;
   int               shift;
   int               BarsHeld;
   bool              newBar;
   datetime          newBarOpenTime;
   datetime          prevBarOpenTime;
   int               currBarOrders;
   bool              candleTraded;
   int               spreadLimit;
   int               maxPyramidTrades;
   int               totalOrders;

   double            holdScore;
   double            bayesianHoldScore;
   double            neuronHoldScore;
   //double            fMSR;
   double            fMSR_Raw;
   double            fMSR_Norm;
   double            fractalAlignment;
   double            microLots;
   double            convictionFactor; // New: Record how much we "bet"
   int               physicsAction;    // New: 1, 0, -1
   double            baseSlope;
   double            consensusThreshold;


   void              freeData() {
      // Properly clear dynamic arrays
      ArrayFree(open);
      ArrayFree(high);
      ArrayFree(low);
      ArrayFree(close);
      ArrayFree(time);
      ArrayFree(tick_volume);
      ArrayFree(std);
      ArrayFree(stdOpen);
      ArrayFree(mfi);
      ArrayFree(obv);
      ArrayFree(rsi);
      ArrayFree(atr);
      ArrayFree(adx);
      ArrayFree(adxPlus);
      ArrayFree(adxMinus);
      ArrayFree(ima5);
      ArrayFree(ima14);
      ArrayFree(ima30);
      ArrayFree(ima60);
      ArrayFree(ima120);
      ArrayFree(ima240);
      ArrayFree(ima500);

      // Reset scalars
      magicnumber = NULL;
      closeProfit = NULL;
      stopLoss = NULL;
      currProfit = NULL;
      maxProfit = NULL;
      shift = NULL;
      currSpread = EMPTY;
      tradePosition = EMPTY;
      BarsHeld = -1;
      newBar = EMPTY;
      holdScore = -1;
      bayesianHoldScore=-1;
      neuronHoldScore=-1;
      fMSR_Raw = EMPTY_VALUE;
      fMSR_Norm = EMPTY_VALUE;;
      fractalAlignment = EMPTY_VALUE;
      microLots = -1;
      convictionFactor = EMPTY_VALUE;
      physicsAction = EMPTY;
      baseSlope = EMPTY_VALUE;
      spreadLimit = EMPTY;
      maxPyramidTrades = EMPTY;
      totalOrders = EMPTY;
      newBarOpenTime = EMPTY;
      prevBarOpenTime = EMPTY;
      candleTraded = EMPTY;
      currBarOrders = EMPTY;
      consensusThreshold = EMPTY_VALUE;
   }

   // Constructor to initialize sizes
                     INDDATA() {
      resize(500,120);
   }

   void              resize(int primaryResize, int secondaryResize) {
      ArrayResize(open, primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(close, primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(tick_volume, primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(ima120, primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(ima240, primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(ima500, primaryResize);
      // Secondary indicators only need 120
      ArrayResize(high, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(low, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(time, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(std, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(stdOpen, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(obv, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(rsi, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(mfi, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(atr, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(adx, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(adxPlus, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(adxMinus, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(ima5, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(ima14, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(ima30, secondaryResize);
      ArrayResize(ima60, secondaryResize);
   }
};



struct SIGBUFF {
   double            buff1[5];
   double            buff2[5];
   double            buff3[5];
   double            buff4[5];
   double            buff5[5];
   double            buff6[5];
   double            buff7[5];
   double            buff8[5];
                     SIGBUFF() {
      initArr();
   }
                    ~SIGBUFF() {
      freeArr();
   }

   void              freeArr() {
      ArrayFree(buff1);
      ArrayFree(buff2);
      ArrayFree(buff3);
      ArrayFree(buff4);
      ArrayFree(buff5);
      ArrayFree(buff6);
      ArrayFree(buff7);
      ArrayFree(buff8);
   }

   void              initArr() {
      ArrayInitialize(buff1, EMPTY_VALUE);
      ArrayInitialize(buff2, EMPTY_VALUE);
      ArrayInitialize(buff3, EMPTY_VALUE);
      ArrayInitialize(buff4, EMPTY_VALUE);
      ArrayInitialize(buff5, EMPTY_VALUE);
      ArrayInitialize(buff6, EMPTY_VALUE);
      ArrayInitialize(buff7, EMPTY_VALUE);
      ArrayInitialize(buff8, EMPTY_VALUE);
   }
   void              resize(int primaryResize) {
      ArrayResize(buff1,primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(buff2,primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(buff3,primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(buff4,primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(buff5,primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(buff6,primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(buff7,primaryResize);
      ArrayResize(buff8,primaryResize);
      initArr();
   }
};

 public:

   SAN_SIGNAL        atrSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        obvCPSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        mfiSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        rsiSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        baseSlopeSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        slope30SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        adxCovDivSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        fastIma514SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        fastIma1430SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        fastIma30120SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        fastIma120240SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        fastIma240500SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        fastIma530SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        ima514SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        ima1430SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        ima30120SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        ima30240SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        ima120240SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        ima120500SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        ima240500SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        ima530SIG;

   SAN_SIGNAL        volSIG;

   SAN_SIGNAL        profitPercentageSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        tradeSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        tradeVolVarSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        lossSIG;
   SANTREND          acfTrendSIG;
   SANTRENDSTRENGTH  acfStrengthSIG;
   SANTREND          trendRatioSIG;
   SANTREND          trendRatio5SIG;
   SANTREND          trendRatio14SIG;
   SANTREND          trendRatio30SIG;
   SANTREND          trendRatio120SIG;
   SANTREND          trendRatio240SIG;
   SANTREND          trendRatio500SIG;
   SANTREND          trendVolRatioSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        trendSumSig;
   SANTRENDSTRENGTH  trendVolRatioStrengthSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        slopeVarSIG;
   SANTREND          trendSlopeSIG;
   SANTREND          trendSlope5SIG;

   SAN_SIGNAL        sig5;

   SIGMAVARIABILITY        cpSDSIG;

   //  DataTransport     imaSlopesData;

};


//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//|                                                                  |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
SANSIGNALS::SANSIGNALS() {
   initBase();
}

//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//|                                                                  |
//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
SANSIGNALS::~SANSIGNALS() {
//hilbertDftSIG.freeData();
   dftSIG.initDTYPE();
   hilbertSIG.initDTYPE();
   clusterData.freeData();
//      imaSlopesData.freeData();
   varDt.freeData();
   slopeRatioData.freeData();
   atrVolData.initDTYPE();
   candleVolData.initDTYPE();
   baseSlopeData.initDTYPE();
   imaSlope5Data.initDTYPE();
   imaSlope14Data.initDTYPE();
   imaSlope30Data.initDTYPE();
   imaSlope60Data.initDTYPE();
   imaSlope120Data.initDTYPE();
   imaSlope500Data.initDTYPE();
   stdCPSlope.initDTYPE();
   stdOPSlope.initDTYPE();
   obvCPSlope.initDTYPE();
   ArrayFree(hilbertAmp);
   ArrayFree(hilbertPhase);
   ArrayFree(dftMag);
   ArrayFree(dftPhase);
   ArrayFree(dftPower);
}

struct SANSIGBOOL {
   bool              spreadBool;
   bool              fimaWaveBool;
   bool              imaWaveBool;
   bool              imaWaveBool1;
   bool              sigBool;
   bool              sigBool1;
   bool              fsigBool;
   bool              signal514Bool;
   bool              signal1430Bool;
   bool              signal5Wave530Bool;
   bool              signal5Wave1430Bool;
   bool              signal5Wave14Bool;
   bool              signal14Wave1430Bool;
   bool              safeSig1Bool;
   bool              safeSig2Bool;
   bool              safeSig3Bool;
   bool              safeSig4Bool;
   bool              safeSig5Bool;
   bool              adxBool;
   bool              adxIma1430Bool;
   bool              atrAdxBool;
   bool              atrAdxVolOpenBool;
   bool              openTradeBool;
   bool              healthyTrendBool;
   bool              healthyTrendStrengthBool;
   bool              flatTrendBool;
   bool              openVolTrendBool;
   bool              closeVolTrendBool;
   bool              imaSig1Bool;
   //bool              cpSDBool;
   //bool              ima5SDBool;
   //bool              ima14SDBool;
   //bool              ima30SDBool;
   //bool              ima120SDBool;
   //bool              imaSDTradeBool;
   //bool              imaSDNoTradeBool;
   //bool              imaSDTradeTradeBool;
   //bool              imaSDNoNoTradeBool;
   bool              starBool;
   bool              candlePipAlarm;


                     SANSIGBOOL() {
      spreadBool = false;
      imaWaveBool = false;
      imaWaveBool1 = false;
      fimaWaveBool = false;
      sigBool = false;
      sigBool1 = false;
      fsigBool = false;
      signal514Bool = false;
      signal1430Bool = false;
      signal5Wave530Bool = false;
      signal5Wave1430Bool = false;
      signal5Wave14Bool = false;
      signal14Wave1430Bool = false;
      safeSig1Bool = false;
      safeSig2Bool = false;
      safeSig3Bool = false;
      safeSig4Bool = false;
      safeSig5Bool = false;
      adxBool = false;
      adxIma1430Bool = false;
      atrAdxBool = false;
      atrAdxVolOpenBool = false;
      imaSig1Bool = false;
      openTradeBool = false;
      healthyTrendBool = false;
      healthyTrendStrengthBool = false;
      flatTrendBool = false;
      openVolTrendBool = false;
      closeVolTrendBool = false;
      //cpSDBool = false;
      //ima5SDBool = false;
      //ima14SDBool = false;
      //ima30SDBool = false;
      //ima120SDBool = false;
      //imaSDTradeBool = false;
      //imaSDTradeTradeBool = false;
      //imaSDNoTradeBool = false;
      //imaSDNoNoTradeBool = false;
      //starBool = false;
      candlePipAlarm = false;
   }
                     SANSIGBOOL(const SANSIGNALS &ss) {
      //spreadBool = (currspread < tl.spreadLimit);
      //      imaWaveBool = ((ss.ima514SIG==ss.ima1430SIG)||(ss.ima530SIG==ss.ima1430SIG)||(ss.ima530SIG==ss.ima514SIG));
      imaWaveBool = ((ss.ima514SIG == ss.ima1430SIG) && (ss.ima1430SIG == ss.ima530_21SIG));
      fimaWaveBool = ((ss.fastIma514SIG == ss.fastIma1430SIG) || (ss.fastIma530SIG == ss.fastIma1430SIG));
      imaWaveBool1 = ((ss.fastIma514SIG == ss.ima514SIG) && ((ss.fastIma1430SIG == ss.ima1430SIG) || (ss.fastIma530SIG == ss.ima530SIG)));
      signal514Bool = (ss.sig5 == ss.sig14);
      signal1430Bool = (ss.sig14 == ss.sig30);
      signal5Wave1430Bool = (ss.sig5 == ss.ima1430SIG);
      signal5Wave530Bool = (ss.sig5 == ss.ima530SIG);
      signal5Wave14Bool = (ss.sig5 == ss.ima514SIG);
      //sigBool = ((signal514Bool && signal1430Bool)||(signal514Bool && (ss.sig5==ss.sig30))) ;
      //fsigBool = ((ss.fsig5==ss.fsig14)&&(ss.fsig14==ss.fsig30));
      sigBool = (signal514Bool && signal1430Bool);
      fsigBool = ((ss.fsig5 == ss.fsig14) && (ss.fsig14 == ss.fsig30));
      sigBool1 = ((ss.fsig5 == ss.sig5) && (ss.fsig14 == ss.sig14) && (ss.fsig30 == ss.sig30));
      signal14Wave1430Bool = (ss.sig14 == ss.ima1430SIG);
      safeSig1Bool = (imaWaveBool && signal5Wave14Bool && (ss.sig5 == ss.ima514SIG));
      safeSig2Bool = (signal14Wave1430Bool);
      safeSig3Bool = (signal5Wave530Bool);
      safeSig4Bool = (sigBool && fsigBool && imaWaveBool && fimaWaveBool && (ss.fsig5 == ss.fastIma514SIG) && (ss.sig5 == ss.ima514SIG) && (ss.fsig5 == ss.sig5) && (ss.fastIma514SIG == ss.ima514SIG));
      adxBool = ((ss.adxSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::BUY) || (ss.adxSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::SELL));
      adxIma1430Bool = (ss.adxSIG == ss.ima1430SIG);
      atrAdxBool = ((ss.atrSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::TRADE) && adxBool);
      atrAdxVolOpenBool = ((ss.volSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::TRADE) && atrAdxBool);
      imaSig1Bool = (spreadBool && safeSig1Bool);
      openTradeBool = (ss.tradeSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::TRADE);
      healthyTrendBool = (((ss.acfTrendSIG != SANTREND::NOTREND) && (ss.acfTrendSIG != SANTREND::FLAT)) || ((ss.trendSlopeSIG != SANTREND::NOTREND) && (ss.trendSlopeSIG != SANTREND::FLAT)));
      healthyTrendStrengthBool = ((ss.acfStrengthSIG != SANTRENDSTRENGTH::WEAK) && (ss.acfStrengthSIG != SANTRENDSTRENGTH::POOR));
      flatTrendBool = ((ss.trendSlopeSIG == SANTREND::FLAT) || ((ss.acfTrendSIG == SANTREND::FLAT) && ((ss.acfStrengthSIG == SANTRENDSTRENGTH::NORMAL) || (ss.acfStrengthSIG == SANTRENDSTRENGTH::HIGH) || (ss.acfStrengthSIG == SANTRENDSTRENGTH::SUPERHIGH))));
      openVolTrendBool = ((ss.volSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::TRADE) && healthyTrendBool && healthyTrendStrengthBool && !flatTrendBool);
      closeVolTrendBool = ((ss.volSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::REVERSETRADE) && !healthyTrendBool && !healthyTrendStrengthBool && flatTrendBool);
      //      cpSDBool = ((ss.cpSDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_NULL)&&(ss.cpSDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_MEAN)&&(ss.cpSDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_MEAN)&&(ss.cpSDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_MEAN)&&(ss.cpSDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_HALF)&&(ss.cpSDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_HALF));
      //      ima5SDBool = ((ss.ima5SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_NULL)&&(ss.ima5SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_MEAN)&&(ss.ima5SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_MEAN)&&(ss.ima5SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_MEAN)&&(ss.ima5SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_HALF)&&(ss.ima5SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_HALF));
      //      ima14SDBool = ((ss.ima14SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_NULL)&&(ss.ima14SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_MEAN)&&(ss.ima14SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_MEAN)&&(ss.ima14SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_MEAN)&&(ss.ima14SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_HALF)&&(ss.ima14SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_HALF));
      //      ima30SDBool = ((ss.ima30SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_NULL)&&(ss.ima30SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_MEAN)&&(ss.ima30SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_MEAN)&&(ss.ima30SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_MEAN)&&(ss.ima30SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_HALF)&&(ss.ima30SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_HALF));
      //      ima120SDBool = ((ss.ima120SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_NULL)&&(ss.ima120SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMA_MEAN)&&(ss.ima120SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_MEAN)&&(ss.ima120SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_MEAN)&&(ss.ima120SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMANEG_HALF)&&(ss.ima120SDSIG!=SIGMAVARIABILITY::SIGMAPOS_HALF));
      //      //ima5SDBool = (ss.ima5SDSIG==SIGMAVARIABILITY::TRADE);
      //      //ima14SDBool = (ss.ima14SDSIG==SIGMAVARIABILITY::TRADE);
      //      //ima30SDBool = (ss.ima30SDSIG==SIGMAVARIABILITY::TRADE);
      //
      //      imaSDTradeBool = (ima14SDBool && ima30SDBool);
      //      imaSDNoTradeBool = (!ima14SDBool && !ima30SDBool);
      //      imaSDTradeTradeBool = (ima5SDBool && ima14SDBool && ima30SDBool);
      //      imaSDNoNoTradeBool = (!ima5SDBool && !ima14SDBool && !ima30SDBool);
      starBool = ((ss.candlePattStarSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::BUY) || (ss.candlePattStarSIG == SAN_SIGNAL::SELL));
   }
                    ~SANSIGBOOL() {}
   void              printStruct() {
      //      Print("cpSDBool: "+cpSDBool+" ima5SDBool: "+ ima5SDBool+" ima14SDBool: "+ ima14SDBool+" ima30DBool: "+ ima30SDBool +" imaSDNoTradeBool: "+imaSDNoTradeBool+" closeVolTrendBool: "+closeVolTrendBool+" openVolTrendBool:"+openVolTrendBool);
      Print("closeVolTrendBool: " + closeVolTrendBool + " openVolTrendBool:" + openVolTrendBool);
      Print("adxBool: " + adxBool + " adxIma1430Bool: " + adxIma1430Bool + " atrAdxBool: " + atrAdxBool + " openTradeBool: " + openTradeBool + " healthyTrendBool:" + healthyTrendBool + " healthyTrendStrengthBool: " + healthyTrendStrengthBool + " atrAdxVolOpenBool: " + atrAdxVolOpenBool + " starBool: " + starBool);
      Print("SpreadBool: " + spreadBool + " imaWaveBool: " + imaWaveBool + " signal514Bool: " + signal514Bool + " signal1430Bool: " + signal1430Bool + " signal5Wave14Bool: " + signal5Wave14Bool + " signal14Wave1430Bool: " + signal14Wave1430Bool + " signal5Wave1430Bool: " + signal5Wave1430Bool + " safeSig1Bool:" + safeSig1Bool + " safeSig2Bool: " + safeSig2Bool + " imaSig1Bool: " + imaSig1Bool);
   }
};

   SAN_SIGNAL        dominantSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        baseSlopeSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        tradeSIG;

   SAN_SIGNAL        tradeSlopeSIG;

   SAN_SIGNAL        candleVolSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        physicsSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        singleCandleVolSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        momSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        c_SIG;

                     T_SIG() {

   }
                    ~T_SIG() {}

   void              initTSIG() {
      dominantSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      baseSlopeSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      tradeSIG=SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      slope30SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      slopeCandle120SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      fastSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      slowSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      atrSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      cp120SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      micWaveSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      macWaveSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;

      waveTideSIG =SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      cpScatterSIG= SANTREND::NOTREND;
      slopeVarSIG=   SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      volMomentumSIG=SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      tradeSlopeSIG=SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      candleVolSIG=SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      physicsSIG=SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      singleCandleVolSIG=SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      momSIG=SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      c_SIG=SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
   }
};

struct STATE_SIGNAL {
   SAN_SIGNAL        dominantSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        c_SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        tradeSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        fastSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        simple_5_14_SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        simple_14_30_SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        simpleTrend_5_14_SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        simpleTrend_14_30_SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        simpleSlope_30_SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        cpSlopeCandle120SIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        volSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        volSlopeSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        dominantTrendCPSIG;
   SAN_SIGNAL        dominantTrendSIG;
   TRADE_STRATEGIES  trdStgy;

   void              initSIG() {
      dominantSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      tradeSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      c_SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      fastSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      simple_5_14_SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      simple_14_30_SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      simpleTrend_5_14_SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      simpleTrend_14_30_SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      simpleSlope_30_SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      cpSlopeCandle120SIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      volSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      volSlopeSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      dominantTrendCPSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      dominantTrendSIG = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      trdStgy = TRADE_STRATEGIES::NOTRDSTGY;
   }

                     STATE_SIGNAL() {
      initSIG();
   }

                    ~STATE_SIGNAL() {
      initSIG();
   }
   void              printState() {
      //Print("[STATE] :: domSIG: "+util.getSigString(dominantSIG)+" c_SIG: "+util.getSigString(c_SIG)+" fastSIG: "+util.getSigString(fastSIG)+" 5_14:"+util.getSigString(simple_5_14_SIG)+" Slope30: "+util.getSigString(simpleSlope_30_SIG)+" cp120: "+util.getSigString(cpSlopeCandle120SIG)+" volSIG:"+ util.getSigString(volSIG)+" volSlopeSIG: "+util.getSigString(volSlopeSIG)+" domTrCP: "+util.getSigString(dominantTrendCPSIG)+" trendSIG:: "+util.getSigString(dominantTrendSIG));
   }
};

struct FEATURE_VECTOR {

// Group A: Momentum & Velocity (The Drivers)
   double            slopeIma5;
   double            slopeIma30;
   double            adxPlusMinusDiff;
   double            rsi;

// Group B: Volatility & Energy (The Fuel)
   double            atr;
   double            stdDevCP;
   double            adx;
   double            tVol;

// Group C: Structure & Stretch (The Geometry)

   double            priceElasticity;
   double            mfi;
   double            vWCM;
   double            expansionCompression;

// Group D: The "Super-Feature" Additions.
   double            bayesianScore;
   double            neuronScore;
   double            fMSR_Norm;
   double            fractalAlignment;


   void              initSIG() {

      slopeIma5 = EMPTY_VALUE;
      slopeIma30 = EMPTY_VALUE;
      adxPlusMinusDiff = EMPTY_VALUE;
      rsi = EMPTY_VALUE;

      atr = EMPTY_VALUE;
      stdDevCP = EMPTY_VALUE;
      adx = EMPTY_VALUE;
      tVol = EMPTY_VALUE;


      priceElasticity = EMPTY_VALUE;
      mfi = EMPTY_VALUE;
      vWCM = EMPTY_VALUE;
      expansionCompression = EMPTY_VALUE;

      bayesianScore = EMPTY_VALUE;
      neuronScore = EMPTY_VALUE;
      fMSR_Norm = EMPTY_VALUE;
      fractalAlignment = EMPTY_VALUE;

   }

                     FEATURE_VECTOR() {
      initSIG();
   }

                    ~FEATURE_VECTOR() {
      initSIG();
   }
   void              printState() {
   }
};

struct STRATEGY_STATE {
   // Candle control
   bool              newCandleGate;      // Replaces per-strategy NEWCANDLE latches
   bool              isNewBar; // simply records the state new bar or not. newCandleGate is to be used for trades
   bool              candleTraded;       // Has a trade been placed this bar?
   int               currBarOrders;
   int               totalOrders;
   // Cross-strategy communication
   SAN_SIGNAL        activeSignal;    // What the strategy decided this tick
   int               strategyId;      // Which strategy is writing this state


   // Debug/tracing
   string            mesg1;         // e.g. "pruneTrades: cut 2 weeds"
   string            mesg2;         // e.g. "pruneTrades: cut 2 weeds"
   string            lastAction;         // e.g. "pruneTrades: cut 2 weeds"
   string            sourceFunction;     // e.g. "imaSt3"
   datetime          stateTimestamp;     // When was state last written


// EA values:

   ulong             magicNumber;
   int               SHIFT;
   int               noOfCandles;
   int               BarsHeld;
   int               activeStrategy;
   int               maxPyramidTrades;
   double            TAKEPROFIT;
   double            STOPLOSS;
   double            TRADEPROFIT;
   double            MAXTRADEPROFIT;
   double            physicsWeight;   // Slightly more voice to Hyperbolic
   double            cobbWeight;// Cobb-Douglas weight (balanced)
   double            cloudWeight;  // Market Cloud weight (conservative)
   double            consensusThreshold;   // Slightly more aggressive

   double            maxMultiplier; // Maximum risk for elite setups
   double            minLotSize;      // Terminal minimum
   double            microLots; // Micro Lots
   double            pipValue;
   bool              g_cbWarmedUp;





                     STRATEGY_STATE() {
      newCandleGate  = false;
      candleTraded   = false;
      currBarOrders  = 0;          // count — 0 means none
      totalOrders    = 0;          // count — 0 means none
      activeSignal   = SAN_SIGNAL::NOSIG;
      strategyId     = 0;          // 0 = not assigned
      mesg1          = "";
      mesg2          = "";
      lastAction     = "";
      sourceFunction = "";
      stateTimestamp = 0;          // datetime — 0 = never written
      SHIFT = 1;
      BarsHeld = 0;
      magicNumber = 1002;
      activeStrategy = 5;
      maxPyramidTrades = 15;
      noOfCandles = 21;
      TAKEPROFIT = 1.4;
      STOPLOSS = 0.3;
      physicsWeight      = 0.48;   // Slightly more voice to Hyperbolic
      cobbWeight         = 0.32;// Cobb-Douglas weight (balanced)
      cloudWeight        = 0.20;  // Market Cloud weight (conservative)
      consensusThreshold = 0.32;   // Slightly more aggressive

      maxMultiplier = 2.0; // Maximum risk for elite setups
      minLotSize = 0.01;      // Terminal minimum
      microLots = 1; // Micro Lots
      pipValue=0;
      g_cbWarmedUp = false;

   }


                    ~STRATEGY_STATE() {}
};


struct DataPointStats {
   int               value;        // -3 to +3
   double            weight;       // 0.1 to 3.0
   double            accuracy;     // 0.0 to 1.0
};


//+------------------------------------------------------------------+
//| CircularBuffer — Fixed-size ring buffer for MQL4                 |
//| Stores the N most recent values, oldest auto-discarded on push   |

//      m_count = m_capacity;

template <typename T>
class CircularBuffer {
 private:

   T                 m_data[];
   int               m_head;
   int               m_count;
   int               m_capacity;

   bool              checkInit(string caller) {
      if(m_capacity <= 0) {
         Print("CircularBuffer::", caller, "() — not initialised");
         return false;
      }
      return true;
   }

 public:
                     CircularBuffer() : m_head(0), m_count(0), m_capacity(0) {}


   void              init(int capacity) {
      if(capacity <= 0) {
         Print("CircularBuffer::init() — capacity must be > 0");
         return;
      }
      m_capacity = capacity;
      m_head     = 0;
      m_count    = 0;
      ArrayResize(m_data, capacity);
   }

   void              push(T value) {
      if(!checkInit("push")) return;
      m_data[m_head] = value;
      m_head = (m_head + 1) % m_capacity;
      if(m_count < m_capacity) m_count++;
   }

   T                 get(int logicalIndex) {
      if(!checkInit("get"))                          return (T)NULL;
      if(m_count == 0)                               return (T)NULL;
      if(logicalIndex < 0 || logicalIndex >= m_count) {
         Print("CircularBuffer::get() — index ", logicalIndex,
               " out of range [0,", m_count-1, "]");
         return (T)NULL;
      }
      int raw = ((m_head - 1 - logicalIndex) + m_capacity) % m_capacity;
      return m_data[raw];
   }

   T                 newest() {
      return get(0);
   }
   T                 oldest() {
      return get(m_count - 1);
   }

   int               count()    {
      return m_count;
   }
   int               capacity() {
      return m_capacity;
   }
   bool              isFull()   {
      return m_count == m_capacity;
   }
   bool              isEmpty()  {
      return m_count == 0;
   }

   void              clear() {
      if(!checkInit("clear")) return;
      m_head  = 0;
      m_count = 0;
   }

   void              destroy() {
      ArrayFree(m_data);
      m_head     = 0;
      m_count    = 0;
      m_capacity = 0;
   }

   // Exports in logical order: index 0 = newest, index N-1 = oldest
   void              exportToArray(T &dest[]) {
      int n = count();
      ArrayResize(dest, n);
      for(int i = 0; i < n; i++)
         dest[i] = get(i);
   }

   void              fill(T value) {
      if(!checkInit("fill")) return;
      for(int i = 0; i < m_capacity; i++) m_data[i] = value;
      m_head  = 0;
      m_count = m_capacity;
   }

   // Updates an existing value at the specified logical index without advancing the buffer
   void              update(int logicalIndex, T value) {
      if(!checkInit("update"))                               return;

      // If buffer is empty, updating index 0 implies we should just push it
      if(m_count == 0 && logicalIndex == 0) {
         push(value);
         return;
      }

      if(logicalIndex < 0 || logicalIndex >= m_count) {
         Print("CircularBuffer::update() — index ", logicalIndex,
               " out of range [0,", m_count-1, "]");
         return;
      }

      // Calculate the raw physical index (exact same math as get() )
      int raw = ((m_head - 1 - logicalIndex) + m_capacity) % m_capacity;
      m_data[raw] = value;
   }

   // Convenience method to update the live candle (Shift 0)
   void              updateNewest(T value) {
      update(0, value);
   }
};

class SignalHistory : public CircularBuffer<SAN_SIGNAL> {
 public:
   // Returns the three numbers fuseProbability() needs
   // derived entirely from the buffer contents
   void              analyse(int &valueOut, double &weightOut, double &accuracyOut) {
      int buys = 0, sells = 0, notrades=0, flips = 0;
      int n = count();

      for(int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
         SAN_SIGNAL s = get(i);
         if(s == BUY)  buys++;
         if(s == SELL) sells++;
         if((s != SAN_SIGNAL::BUY)&&(s != SAN_SIGNAL::SELL)) notrades++;
         // flip = signal changed from previous (i+1 is one older)
         if(i < n-1) {
            SAN_SIGNAL prev = get(i+1);
            if(s != prev && s != NOSIG && prev != NOSIG)
               flips++;
         }
      }

      int total     = buys + sells;
      if((total == 0)||(buys == sells)) {
         valueOut=0;
         weightOut=0.1;
         accuracyOut=0.5;
         return;
      }

      // True 7-level output: -3,-2,-1, 0, +1,+2,+3
      //if(total == 0) {
      //   valueOut = 0;
      //   return;   // no data — abstain
      //}

      //if(buys == sells) {
      //   valueOut = 0;
      //   return;   // perfect tie — abstain
      //}

      int    dominant   = MathMax(buys, sells);
      double biasRatio  = (double)dominant / total;
      double consistency = 1.0 - (double)flips / MathMax(total - 1, 1);
      int    direction  = (sells > buys) ? -1 : +1;

      // magnitude from bias
      int magnitude = (biasRatio >= 0.75) ? 3 :
                      (biasRatio >= 0.60) ? 2 : 1;

      valueOut    = direction * magnitude;
      weightOut   = 0.5 + (consistency * 2.5);          // [0.5, 3.0]
      accuracyOut = 0.5 + (biasRatio - 0.5) * 0.5;     // [0.5, 0.75]
   }

// Notice the * instead of &
   double            calculateAgreement(SignalHistory *otherBuffer) {
      if(CheckPointer(otherBuffer) == POINTER_INVALID) return 0.5; // Safety first!
      if(this.count() != otherBuffer.count() || this.count() == 0) return 0.5;

      int n = count();
      int matches = 0;
      int validComparisons = 0;

      for(int i = 0; i < n; i++) {
         SAN_SIGNAL sigA = this.get(i);
         SAN_SIGNAL sigB = otherBuffer.get(i); // Dot operator is correct in MQL4!

         if(sigA != NOSIG && sigB != NOSIG) {
            validComparisons++;
            if(sigA == sigB) matches++;
         }
      }

      if(validComparisons == 0) return 0.5;

      double rawAgreement = (double)matches / validComparisons;
      return MathAbs(rawAgreement - 0.5) * 2.0;
   }
};



struct INDDATA_CB {
   CircularBuffer<double> open;
   CircularBuffer<double> high;
   CircularBuffer<double> low;
   CircularBuffer<double> close;
   CircularBuffer<datetime> time;
   CircularBuffer<double> tick_volume;
   CircularBuffer<double> std;
   CircularBuffer<double> stdOpen;
   CircularBuffer<double> mfi;
   CircularBuffer<double> obv;
   CircularBuffer<double> rsi;
   CircularBuffer<double> atr;
   CircularBuffer<double> adx;
   CircularBuffer<double> adxPlus;
   CircularBuffer<double> adxMinus;
   CircularBuffer<double> ima5;
   CircularBuffer<double> ima14;
   CircularBuffer<double> ima30;
   CircularBuffer<double> ima60;
   CircularBuffer<double> ima120;
   CircularBuffer<double> ima240;
   CircularBuffer<double> ima500;
   ulong             magicnumber;
   double            closeProfit; // Profit at which a trade is condsidered for closing. Also the same as take profit
   double            stopLoss; // Stop Loss
   double            currProfit; // The profit of the currently held trade
   double            maxProfit; // The current profit is adjusted by subtracting the spread and a margin added.
   int               tradePosition;
   int               currSpread;
   int               shift;
   int               BarsHeld;
   bool              newBar;
   datetime          newBarOpenTime;
   datetime          prevBarOpenTime;
   int               currBarOrders;
   bool              candleTraded;
   int               spreadLimit;
   int               maxPyramidTrades;
   int               totalOrders;

   double            holdScore;
   double            bayesianHoldScore;
   double            neuronHoldScore;
   //double            fMSR;
   double            fMSR_Raw;
   double            fMSR_Norm;
   double            fractalAlignment;
   double            microLots;
   double            convictionFactor; // New: Record how much we "bet"
   int               physicsAction;    // New: 1, 0, -1
   double            baseSlope;
   double            consensusThreshold;


   void              freeData() {
      // Properly clear dynamic arrays
      open.destroy();
      high.destroy();
      low.destroy();
      close.destroy();
      time.destroy();
      tick_volume.destroy();
      std.destroy();
      stdOpen.destroy();
      mfi.destroy();
      obv.destroy();
      rsi.destroy();
      atr.destroy();
      adx.destroy();
      adxPlus.destroy();
      adxMinus.destroy();
      ima5.destroy();
      ima14.destroy();
      ima30.destroy();
      ima60.destroy();
      ima120.destroy();
      ima240.destroy();
      ima500.destroy();

      // Reset scalars
      magicnumber = NULL;
      closeProfit = NULL;
      stopLoss = NULL;
      currProfit = NULL;
      maxProfit = NULL;
      shift = NULL;
      currSpread = EMPTY;
      tradePosition = EMPTY;
      BarsHeld = -1;
      newBar = EMPTY;
      holdScore = -1;
      bayesianHoldScore=-1;
      neuronHoldScore=-1;
      fMSR_Raw = EMPTY_VALUE;
      fMSR_Norm = EMPTY_VALUE;;
      fractalAlignment = EMPTY_VALUE;
      microLots = -1;
      convictionFactor = EMPTY_VALUE;
      physicsAction = EMPTY;
      baseSlope = EMPTY_VALUE;
      spreadLimit = EMPTY;
      maxPyramidTrades = EMPTY;
      totalOrders = EMPTY;
      newBarOpenTime = EMPTY;
      prevBarOpenTime = EMPTY;
      candleTraded = EMPTY;
      currBarOrders = EMPTY;
      consensusThreshold = EMPTY_VALUE;
   }

   // Constructor to initialize sizes
                     INDDATA_CB() {
      resize(500,120);
   }

   void              resize(int primaryResize, int secondaryResize) {
      open.init(primaryResize);
      close.init(primaryResize);
      tick_volume.init(primaryResize);
      ima120.init(primaryResize);
      ima240.init(primaryResize);
      ima500.init(primaryResize);

      high.init(secondaryResize);
      low.init(secondaryResize);
      time.init(secondaryResize);
      std.init(secondaryResize);
      stdOpen.init(secondaryResize);

      obv.init(secondaryResize);
      rsi.init(secondaryResize);
      mfi.init(secondaryResize);
      atr.init(secondaryResize);
      adx.init(secondaryResize);
      adxPlus.init(secondaryResize);
      adxMinus.init(secondaryResize);
      ima5.init(secondaryResize);
      ima14.init(secondaryResize);
      ima30.init(secondaryResize);
      ima60.init(secondaryResize);
   }
};
